## Documentation For Authorization

## BearerToken
- **Type**: API key 

Example
```
	auth := context.WithValue(context.TODO(), sw.ContextAPIKey, sw.APIKey{
		Key: "APIKEY",
		Prefix: "Bearer", // Omit if not necessary.
	})
    r, err := client.Service.Operation(auth, args)
```
